{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","title":"Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken (Paleo, Whole30, Keto)","link":"https://nomnompaleo.com/2016/08/07/pressure-cooker-summer-italian-chicken/","description":"<p><i>Keep your house cool in the summertime by making this delicious and super simple&nbsp;keto- and Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! It’s a quick blast of summer, &nbsp;with tender chicken, juicy cherry tomatoes, fragrant fresh herbs, and buttery, briny green olives.</i></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19694\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/IP-Summer-Italian-Chicken-2-800.jpg\" alt=\"A ladle placing Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken into a light blue bowl. The red banner at the bottom states that the dish is paleo, Whole30, keto, and gluten-free.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/IP-Summer-Italian-Chicken-2-800.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/IP-Summer-Italian-Chicken-2-800-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/IP-Summer-Italian-Chicken-2-800-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/IP-Summer-Italian-Chicken-2-800-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Instant Pot Keeps Your House Cool!</h2> \n<p>One of my favorite cooking appliances to use in the summer is my handy dandy <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/instant-pot-deals\">Instant Pot</a>. &nbsp;At the end of a hot summer day, I’m sweaty and tired, and in no mood to cook.</p> \n<p>Thankfully, I’ve got this wonder appliance!&nbsp;With this indispensable electric pressure cooker, I can throw in a bunch of seasonal ingredients and <i>presto change-o!</i>: a flavor-packed dinner is ready in no time at all, and my kitchen stays cool. Plus, you can take advantage of summer produce and make this fantastic Italian chicken stew in a flash!</p> \n<p>Want more Instant Pot recipes? I’ve got ’em all right <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/125878339293/my-top-paleo-pressure-cookerinstant-pot-recipes\">here</a>!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8518 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaaaPressureCookerDSC_9447-w750.jpg\" alt=\"An Asian woman is using tongs to stir Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken while a small boy watches.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaaaPressureCookerDSC_9447-w750.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaaaPressureCookerDSC_9447-w750-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaaaPressureCookerDSC_9447-w750-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Can you use other Chicken Parts?</h2> \n<p>As always, I highly recommend that you use chicken thighs instead of boneless, skinless chicken breasts because they won’t dry out as easily. Plus, chicken thighs simply taste better (see Exhibit A: <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/74180911762/cracklin-chicken\">Cracklin’ Chicken</a>).</p> \n<p>But yes, you can definitely use other chicken parts and my recipe below has cooking times for boneless chicken breasts, drumsticks, bone-in thighs, etc.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-12153 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/iwL5aihg.jpeg\" alt=\"A collage of the cooking steps to make Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken, a Whole30-friendly weeknight stew.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/iwL5aihg.jpeg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/iwL5aihg-200x300.jpeg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/iwL5aihg-768x1152.jpeg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/iwL5aihg-750x1125.jpeg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Do you need to add extra liquid?</h2> \n<p>Nope! Everyone always asks me why I don’t add at least a cup of liquid to this Instant Pot recipe and it’s because it’s not necessary—the mushrooms, onions, cherry tomatoes, and chicken release enough liquid for the contents to reach high pressure. Adding extra liquid will only dilute the flavors more. Trust me!</p> \n<h2>What can you serve with it?</h2> \n<p>This summer stew tastes great ladled over <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/1626071845/another-simpler-version-of-cauliflower-rice\">Cauliflower Rice</a>, <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/131794514903/pressure-cooker-spaghetti-squash\">Instant Pot Spaghetti Squash</a>, or <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/1356203768/garlic-cauliflower-mashed-potatoes\">Garlic Cauliflower Mashed “Potatoes.</a>” I also love to serve it with a big green salad, <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/roasted-green-beans-with-lemon-and-garlic\">Roasted Green Beans with Lemon and Garlic</a> or <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/138166087728/whole-roasted-cauliflower\">Whole Roasted Cauliflower</a>. You can totally toss it with gluten-free pasta or even regular pasta—your secret is safe with me!</p> \n<h2>Can you make this in a slow cooker or on the stove?</h2> \n<p>Yep! If you are cooking this Italian chicken stew in the slow cooker, sauté the veggies in a skillet before transferring it to the slow cooker. Then, add the rest of the ingredients and cook on low for 2 to 4 hours.</p> \n<p>Making it on the stove? Cook everything in a large sauce pan or deep skillet and simmer covered for about 30 minutes or until the chicken thighs reach 165°F and are tender. (Chicken breasts will cook quicker, so start checking them at the 20 min mark.)</p> \n<h2>Time to make Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken!</h2> \n<p>\n <!-- more --></p> \n<p><i>Serves 6</i></p> \n<p><b>Ingredients</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li>8 boneless skinless chicken thighs</li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2aDiP5C\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Kosher salt</a></li> \n <li>1 tablespoon <a href=\"http://amzn.to/2aM4ODy\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">ghee</a>, avocado oil, or olive oil</li> \n <li>1 small onion, coarsely chopped</li> \n <li>2 medium carrots, coarsely chopped</li> \n <li>½ pound cremini mushrooms, stemmed and quartered</li> \n <li>3 garlic cloves, peeled and smashed</li> \n <li>1 tablespoon <a href=\"http://amzn.to/2aDjMdZ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">tomato paste</a></li> \n <li>2 cups cherry tomatoes</li> \n <li>½ cup pitted green olives (I love Castelvetrano olives)</li> \n <li>¼ teaspoon freshly cracked black pepper</li> \n <li>½ cup loosely packed fresh basil leaves, thinly sliced</li> \n <li>¼ cup loosely packed fresh Italian parsley, coarsely chopped</li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Equipment</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li>All of my recommended kitchen tools are listed <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/shop/nomnompaleo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\"><strong>here</strong></a>.</li> \n <li>My favorite Instant Pot models are listed <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/instant-pot-deals\"><strong>here</strong></a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Method</b></p> \n<p>Grab your chicken thighs and sprinkle ¾ teaspoons kosher salt all over them. You can do this part up to two days in advance, and keep the chicken covered in the fridge.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8520 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick01.jpg\" alt=\"Someone is sprinkling kosher salt on boneless, skinless chicken thighs to make Whole30 Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken stew\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick01.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick01-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick01-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Press the “Sauté” button on the Instant Pot or heat a stovetop pressure cooker over medium heat. Add your fat of choice.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8521 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick02.jpg\" alt=\"A finger is pressing the Sauté button on an Instant Pot to make Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken stew\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick02.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick02-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick02-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>When the fat is shimmering, add the onions, carrots, and mushrooms, and a ½ teaspoon kosher salt.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8522 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick03.jpg\" alt=\"A hand is adding the vegetables to an open Instant Pot to make paleo Summer Italian Chicken stew\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick03.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick03-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick03-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Sauté the vegetables until the softened, about 3 to 5 minutes.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8523 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick04.jpg\" alt=\"Sauteing the vegetables in an open Instant Pot to make Whole30 Summer Italian Chicken \" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick04.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick04-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick04-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Stir in the garlic and tomato paste, and cook for about 30 seconds or until fragrant.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8524 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick05.jpg\" alt=\"Sauteeing the ingredients of Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken with some tomato paste.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick05.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick05-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick05-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Add the salted chicken, cherry tomatoes and green olives to the pot.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8525 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick06.jpg\" alt=\"Adding the chicken thighs, cherry tomatoes, and green olives to an instant pot.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick06.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick06-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick06-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Give it all a good stir.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8526 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick07.jpg\" alt=\"A person is stirring the raw ingredients for the Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken stew before putting on the lid.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick07.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick07-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick07-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Turn off the sauté function, and lock the lid on the pressure cooker.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8527 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick08.jpg\" alt=\"A finer is pressing the Keep Warm/Cancel button on an Instant Pot \" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick08.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick08-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick08-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>I position my Instant Pot under my stovetop exhaust vent before I program the pressure cooking so that when the chicken’s done and I immediately release the pressure, the vent will suck up all the steam. Your kitchen cabinets will thank you. (Stick a cutting board underneath your cooker if your stovetop grates aren’t even—and remember not to turn on your stove!)</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8528 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick09.jpg\" alt=\"A person is putting an Instant Pot filled with Summer Italian Chicken stew under a vent.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick09.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick09-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick09-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>If you’re using an Instant Pot, press the “Manual” or “Pressure Cook” button and set the cooking time at 10 minutes for boneless thighs. Other chicken cuts? Program 7 minutes under high pressure for boneless chicken breasts (if your chicken boobs are bigger than 8 ounces each, you can cut them in half or increase the cooking time to 9 minutes) and 15 minutes under high pressure for bone-in thighs and drumsticks.</p> \n<p>(For those of you using a stovetop pressure cooker, crank the heat to high to bring the contents to high pressure. Once high pressure is reached, reduce the heat to low, or just enough to maintain high pressure. Set a timer for 6 minutes for breasts and 9 minutes for thighs.)</p> \n<p>When the chicken is finished cooking, turn on the stovetop exhaust fan before turning the pressure cooker valve to release the steam.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8529 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick10.jpg\" alt=\"A hand is manually releasing the pressure on an Instant Pot.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick10.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick10-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick10-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Remove the lid right away to prevent overcooking. Add the freshly cracked black pepper and adjust the seasoning with additional salt as needed.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8530 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick11.jpg\" alt=\"A woman is opens and Instant Pot with lots of steam coming out, and adds freshly cracked black pepper\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick11.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick11-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick11-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>If you want a thicker gravy, remove the chicken and blend up the vegetables and cooking liquid with an immersion blender. Personally, I don’t have time for this step. BECAUSE I’M HOT AND TIRED, REMEMBER?</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8531 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick12.jpg\" alt=\"An open Instant Pot filled with Whole30 Summer Italian Chicken stew.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick12.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick12-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick12-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Stir in the fresh herbs, and serve immediately.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8532 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick13.jpg\" alt=\"A hand is adding minced fresh herbs to the Instant Pot.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick13.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick13-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick13-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Wondering what to serve with this?&nbsp;This stew tastes great ladled over <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/1626071845/another-simpler-version-of-cauliflower-rice\">cauliflower rice</a> or <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/1356203768/garlic-cauliflower-mashed-potatoes\">garlic cauliflower mashed “potatoes.”</a></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8533 size-large\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick14-800x1200.jpg\" alt=\"A hand is ladling Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken into a serving bowl.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick14.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick14-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick14-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick14-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Or just eat it as-is if you don’t want to dirty any other pots or pans.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8519 size-large\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick00-800x1200.jpg\" alt=\"A hand is spooning Whole30, keto, Paleo Instant Pot Summer Italian Chicken out of a serving bowl.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" data-pin-description=\"You can keep your house cool in the summer by making this delicious and super simple Whole30-friendly Instant Pot Summer Italian chicken stew! #paleo #nomnompaleo #instantpot #chickenstew #whole30 #glutenfree\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick00.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick00-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick00-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800InstantPotSummerItalianChickenaPCitalchick00-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Toss any leftovers (covered, of course) in the fridge for up to 4 days or in the freezer for up to 6 months.</p> \n<p>Want more Instant Pot recipes? I’ve got ’em all right <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/125878339293/my-top-paleo-pressure-cookerinstant-pot-recipes\">here</a>!</p> \n<p>[Originally posted on August 7, 2016. aria-label=\"Change unit system to Metric\">Metric</a>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Instructions</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-group\">\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions\">\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-0\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Grab your chicken thighs and sprinkle ¾ teaspoons kosher salt all over them. You can do this part up to two days in advance, and keep the chicken covered in the fridge.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-1\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Press the \"Sauté\" button on the Instant Pot or heat a stovetop pressure cooker over medium heat. Add your fat of choice.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-2\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">When the fat is shimmering, add the onions, carrots, and mushrooms, and a ½ teaspoon kosher salt. Sauté the vegetables until the softened, about 3 to 5 minutes.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-3\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Stir in the garlic and tomato paste, and cook for about 30 seconds or until fragrant.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-4\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Add the salted chicken, cherry tomatoes and green olives to the pot.&nbsp;Give it all a good stir.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-5\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Turn off the sauté function, and lock the lid on the pressure cooker.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-6\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">If you’re using an Instant Pot, press the “Manual” or “Pressure Cook” button and set the cooking time at 10 minutes for boneless thighs. Other chicken cuts? Program 7 minutes under high pressure for boneless chicken breasts (if your chicken boobs are bigger than 8 ounces each, you can cut them in half or increase the cooking time to 9 minutes) and 15 minutes under high pressure for bone-in thighs and drumsticks.</span>\n       <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div>\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">(For those of you using a stovetop pressure cooker, crank the heat to high to bring the contents to high pressure. Once high pressure is reached, reduce the heat to low, or just enough to maintain high pressure. Set a timer for 6 minutes for breasts and 9 minutes for thighs.)</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-7\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">When the chicken is finished cooking, release the pressure manually.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-8\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Remove the lid right away to prevent overcooking. Add the freshly cracked black pepper and adjust the seasoning with additional salt as needed.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-9\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       If you want a thicker gravy, remove the chicken and blend up the vegetables and cooking liquid with an immersion blender.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-10\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Stir in the fresh herbs, and serve immediately.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-4777-step-0-11\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Toss any leftovers (covered, of course) in the fridge for up to 4 days or in the freezer for up to 6 months.\n      </div></li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div id=\"wprm-recipe-video-container-4777\" class=\"wprm-recipe-video-container\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-video-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Video</h3>\n   <div \n    </div> \n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-notes-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-notes-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Notes</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-notes\">\n    <ul> \n     <li><span data-slate-fragment=\"JTVCJTdCJTIydHlwZSUyMiUzQSUyMnBhcmFncmFwaCUyMiUyQyUyMmNoaWxkcmVuJTIyJTNBJTVCJTdCJTIydGV4dCUyMiUzQSUyMkklMjBwb3NpdGlvbiUyMG15JTIwSW5zdGFudCUyMFBvdCUyMHVuZGVyJTIwbXklMjBzdG92ZXRvcCUyMGV4aGF1c3QlMjB2ZW50JTIwYmVmb3JlJTIwSSUyMHByb2dyYW0lMjB0aGUlMjBwcmVzc3VyZSUyMGNvb2tpbmclMjBzbyUyMHRoYXQlMjB3aGVuJTIwdGhlJTIwY2hpY2tlbiVFMiU4MCU5OXMlMjBkb25lJTIwYW5kJTIwSSUyMGltbWVkaWF0ZWx5JTIwcmVsZWFzZSUyMHRoZSUyMHByZXNzdXJlJTJDJTIwdGhlJTIwdmVudCUyMHdpbGwlMjBzdWNrJTIwdXAlMjBhbGwlMjB0aGUlMjBzdGVhbS4lMjBZb3VyJTIwa2l0Y2hlbiUyMGNhYmluZXRzJTIwd2lsbCUyMHRoYW5rJTIweW91LiUyMChTdGljayUyMGElMjBjdXR0aW5nJTIwYm9hcmQlMjB1bmRlcm5lYXRoJTIweW91ciUyMGNvb2tlciUyMGlmJTIweW91ciUyMHN0b3ZldG9wJTIwZ3JhdGVzJTIwYXJlbiVFMiU4MCU5OXQlMjBldmVuJUUyJTgwJTk0YW5kJTIwcmVtZW1iZXIlMjBub3QlMjB0byUyMHR1cm4lMjBvbiUyMHlvdXIlMjBzdG92ZSEpJTIyJTdEJTVEJTdEJTVE\">I position my Instant Pot under my stovetop exhaust vent before I program the pressure cooking so that when the chicken’s done and I immediately release the pressure, the vent will suck up all the steam. Your kitchen cabinets will thank you. (Stick a cutting board underneath your cooker if your stovetop grates aren’t even—and remember not to turn on your stove!)</span></li> \n     <li><span data-slate-fragment=\"JTVCJTdCJTIydHlwZSUyMiUzQSUyMnBhcmFncmFwaCUyMiUyQyUyMmNoaWxkcmVuJTIyJTNBJTVCJTdCJTIydGV4dCUyMiUzQSUyMldoZW4lMjB0aGUlMjBjaGlja2VuJTIwaXMlMjBmaW5pc2hlZCUyMGNvb2tpbmclMkMlMjB0dXJuJTIwb24lMjB0aGUlMjBzdG92ZXRvcCUyMGV4aGF1c3QlMjBmYW4lMjBiZWZvcmUlMjB0dXJuaW5nJTIwdGhlJTIwcHJlc3N1cmUlMjBjb29rZXIlMjB2YWx2ZSUyMHRvJTIwcmVsZWFzZSUyMHRoZSUyMHN0ZWFtLiUyMiU3RCU1RCU3RCU1RA==\">When the chicken is finished cooking, turn on the stovetop exhaust fan before turning the pressure cooker valve to release the steam.</span></li> \n    </ul>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <h3 07:01:25","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","title":"Paleo Shrimp Tacos (Whole30, Keto)","link":"https://nomnompaleo.com/?p=7718","description":"<p><em>Raise your hands if you’re hungry for some Whole30-friendly Paleo Shrimp Tacos!&nbsp;This quick and healthy weeknight supper is a cinch to throw together!</em></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19440\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Paleo-Shrimp-Tacos-800.jpeg\" alt=\"A closeup of Paleo Shrimp Tacos on a bed of lettuce and topped with Avocado Crema. The red label says paleo, gluten-free, and keto.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Paleo-Shrimp-Tacos-800.jpeg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Paleo-Shrimp-Tacos-800-200x300.jpeg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Paleo-Shrimp-Tacos-800-768x1152.jpeg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Paleo-Shrimp-Tacos-800-750x1125.jpeg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Tired of &nbsp;Ground Beef Tacos?</h2> \n<p>When I was little, I somehow got the idea that all tacos consisted of ground beef served in crispy, fried taco shells. As a suburban child of the ’70s and ’80s, I naturally assumed that all tacos looked just like the crunchy variety from Taco Bell. (Believe it or not, <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tlQ6RzAtPpM\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">Taco Bell didn’t introduce soft tacos until 1987</a>, when I was already a teenager.) When my Aunt Elaine would make tacos at home, she went even further: She’d stuff seasoned ground meat into soft corn tortillas, and then seal ’em tight and DEEP FRY THE WHOLE THING. (They were delicious, by the way.) To me, tacos = fried corn shells and meat.</p> \n<p>It wasn’t until I was in high school that a friend took me to an authentic Mexican taqueria, where I saw—and tasted—the incredible variety of tacos available. There weren’t just “ground beef tacos” on the menu; you could choose from <em>carne asada</em>,&nbsp;<em>cabeza</em>, and <em>lengua</em>. And beef wasn’t the only option, either. There was <em>tinga de pollo</em>, <em>carnitas</em>, and even <em>camarones</em>—SHRIMP!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7710\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0489.jpg\" alt=\"Closeup up two cooked shrimp on a lettuce leaf next to a slice of lime.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0489.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0489-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0489-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Healthy Weeknight Shrimp Tacos!</h2> \n<p>Over the years, shrimp tacos have become a favorite in our family. We make ’em whenever we crave the bright, fresh combination of shrimp, lime, and avocado (which is, admittedly, all the time). These shrimp tacos are Paleo, Keto, and Whole30-friendly, too) because we substitute butter lettuce leaves for the tortillas—but to be honest, with these tacos, we never miss the tortillas anyway. Soft or crispy, the tortillas would just mask the brilliant, zesty flavors of these Paleo Shrimp Tacos.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-7711 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0766.jpg\" alt=\"Paleo shrimp tacos in a bed of lettuce sitting on a plate with slices of lime. Surrounding the plate is a bowl of guacamole and a bowl of chopped onions.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" data-pin-description=\"\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0766.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0766-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0766-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0766-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Use frozen shrimp!</h2> \n<p>I always stock up on frozen shrimp for weeknight dinner emergencies because you can quickly thaw them in about 5 to 10 minutes. Simply throw the frozen shrimp into a colander and run lukewarm water on them until the shrimp thaw, tossing them every so often. Then, blot the thawed shrimp dry with paper towels and continue with the recipe!</p> \n<p>Buying high quality shrimp can be confusing so I always refer to the <a href=\"https://www.seafoodwatch.org/seafood-recommendations/groups/shrimp/overview?q=Shrimp&amp;t=shrimp\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">Seafood Watch Program guide</a>&nbsp;to steer me in the right direction.</p> \n<h2>How to cook them on a grill</h2> \n<p>Although I usually cook these shrimp tacos on a sheet pan in the oven, I prefer to throw them on the grill in the summertime!</p> \n<h3>On a Traeger Grill</h3> \n<p>If you’ve got a Traeger grill, you can use it like an outdoor oven and throw the sheet pan of marinated shrimp in it. I’ve learned through some trial and error that my oven recipes can cook in a Traeger, but you need to increase the temperature by about 25°F (i.e. for this recipe, cook in the Traeger at 425°F for 6 to 8 minutes or until just cooked through). For those of you wondering, I own and highly recommend&nbsp;<a href=\"https://amzn.to/3d9gkrD\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">this Traeger model</a>.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3>On a Gas Grill</h3> \n<p>Got a gas grill? Soak some bamboo skewers in water for 30 minutes. Grab a skewer and thread about 6 to 8 shrimp on it. &nbsp;Repeat the process until all the shrimp are skewered.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Crank the burners on the gas grill to high, cover, and heat until super hot. Then, scrape the grates clean and oil with avocado oil. Place the skewers on the grill and cook covered for 3 to 4 minutes, before flipping and cooking for 2 to 3 more minutes or until pink and just cooked through.</p> \n<h2>Air Fryer Cooking Instructions</h2> \n<p>Yes, you can cook the shrimp in an air fryer! Heat the air fryer to 400°F and place the shrimp in a single layer in the cooking basket. Air-fry for 5 to 7 minutes or until pink and just cooked through. You may need to cook the shrimp in batches if the basket is small.</p> \n<h2>What can you serve with the Shrimp Tacos?</h2> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/mexi-cauli-rice\">Mexi-Cauli Rice (Mexican Cauliflower Rice)</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/mexican-watermelon-salad\">Mexican Watermelon Salad</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/spicy-mango-cabbage-slaw\">Spicy Mango Cabbage Slaw</a></li> \n</ul> \n<h2>Time to make Paleo Shrimp Tacos!</h2> \n<p><em>Serves 4</em></p> \n<p><strong>Ingredients:</strong></p> \n<p><em>For the Paleo Shrimp Tacos:</em></p> \n<ul> \n <li>¼ cup avocado or olive oil</li> \n <li>3 tablespoons fresh oregano, minced (or 1 tablespoon dried oregano)</li> \n <li>2 garlic cloves, minced</li> \n <li>Zest from one lime</li> \n <li>1½ pounds peeled and deveined shrimp (21-25 count)</li> \n <li>1 small white onion, peeled and finely diced</li> \n <li>¼ cup cilantro, minced</li> \n <li>½ teaspoon <a href=\"http://amzn.to/2mz93t7\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Diamond Crystal brand kosher salt</a></li> \n <li>¼ teaspoon freshly ground black pepper</li> \n <li>1 head butter lettuce, leaves separated</li> \n <li>1 lime, cut into wedges</li> \n</ul> \n<p><em>For the Avocado Crema:</em></p> \n<ul> \n <li>1 large Hass avocado</li> \n <li>¼ cup full-fat coconut milk</li> \n <li>2 tablespoons cilantro, roughly chopped</li> \n <li>¼ cup chives, roughly chopped</li> \n <li>2 tablespoons freshly squeezed lime juice</li> \n <li>½ teaspoon kosher salt</li> \n <li>¼ teaspoon freshly ground black pepper</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Equipment:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>All of my recommended kitchen tools are listed <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/shop/nomnompaleo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\"><strong>here</strong></a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Method:</strong></p> \n<p>In a bowl, stir together the oil, oregano, garlic, and lime zest.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7713\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9658.jpg\" alt=\"In a small bowl, someone is stirring the sauce for the paleo shrimp tacos.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9658.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9658-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9658-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Toss in the shrimp.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7714\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9684.jpg\" alt=\"Someone is adding raw shrimp to a bowl of marinade to make paleo, Whole30, and keto shrimp tacos.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9684.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9684-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9684-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Mix well, making sure that the shrimp is evenly covered. Refrigerate for 30 minutes or up to 2 hours.&nbsp;(No time to marinate the shrimp? It’ll still taste good!)</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7715\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9720.jpg\" alt=\"Someone is mixing by hand the shrimp in the bowl of marinade.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9720.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9720-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9720-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Combine the diced white onion and minced cilantro in a small bowl, and refrigerate until ready to serve.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-7705 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0128.jpg\" alt=\"Someone stirring in a small bowl diced onions with chopped cilantro.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0128.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0128-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0128-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Next, make the Avocado Crema. (Psst! This is the same Avocado Crema that I make for my <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/20170613sheet-pan-chicken-fajitas-avocado-crema\">Sheet Pan Chicken Fajitas</a>!) Cut the avocado in half lengthwise and remove the seed. Scoop the flesh into a food processor or blender. Add the coconut milk, cilantro, chives, lime juice, salt, and pepper.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7717\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9935.jpg\" alt=\"The ingredients coconut milk, cilantro, chives, lime juice, salt, and pepper for dairy-free avocado crema in a high speed blender.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9935.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9935-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_9935-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Blitz until smooth. Add some water to thin out the sauce if desired.Taste and adjust the seasoning as needed with salt, pepper, or more lime juice. You can refrigerate the crema in a container for up to 2 days.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7703\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0008.jpg\" alt=\"Dairy-free and paleo avocado crema in a high speed blender mixed.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0008.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0008-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0008-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>When you’re ready to cook the shrimp, set the oven to 400°F with the rack in the middle position. Toss the shrimp with the salt and black pepper. Then, arrange the shrimp in a single layer on a parchment-lined baking sheet.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7706\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0186.jpg\" alt=\"Someone placing the marinated shrimp in rows on a parchment lined baking sheet.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0186.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0186-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0186-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Pop it in the oven.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7707\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0202.jpg\" alt=\"Someone placing the paleo shrimp on a baking sheet into the oven.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0202.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0202-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0202-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Roast for 6 to 8 minutes or until the shrimp is cooked through.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7708\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0288.jpg\" alt=\"Paleo shrimp roasted in the oven on a parchment-lined baking sheet, lightly cooked and slightly pink.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0288.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0288-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0288-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Arrange the shrimp on lettuce leaves (a.k.a. nature’s tortillas!) and top with the diced onion and cilantro mixture and lime wedges.&nbsp;Drizzle or squirt avocado crema on the tacos.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7709\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0392.jpg\" alt=\"Someone squeezing a bottle filled with paleo and dairy-free avocado crema on top of the paleo shrimp tacos.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0392.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0392-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0392-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Ta-da! Paleo Shrimp Tacos—and they’re perfect for your Whole30, too!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7712\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0774a.jpg\" alt=\"An overhead shot of paleo shrimp tacos on butter lettuce with cilantro, onions, and lime.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0774a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0774a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800ShrimpTacosaaDSC_0774a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>[Originally posted on January 15, 2018. Updated with new details and photos on June 15, 2020.]</p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<p><em>Looking for more recipe ideas? target=\"_blank\">Michelle Tam</a></span>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredients-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-ingredients-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Ingredients</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-group\">\n    <h4 class=\"wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name wprm-block-text-bold\">For the Paleo Shrimp Tacos:</h4>\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredients\">\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">¼</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">cup</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">avocado or olive oil</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">3</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">tablespoons</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">fresh oregano</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">minced (or 1 tablespoon dried oregano)</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">2</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">garlic cloves</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">minced</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">Zest from one lime</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">1½</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">pounds</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">peeled and deveined shrimp</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">21-25 count</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">1</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">small white onion</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">peeled and finely diced</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">¼</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">cup</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">cilantro</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">minced</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">½</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">teaspoon</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\"><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2mz93t7\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Diamond Crystal brand kosher salt</a></span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">¼</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">teaspoon</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">freshly ground black pepper</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">1</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">head butter lettuce</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">leaves separated</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">1</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">lime</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">cut into wedges</span></li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-group\">\n    <h4 class=\"wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name wprm-block-text-bold\">For the Avocado Crema:</h4>\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredients\">\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">1</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">large Hass avocado</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">¼</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">cup</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\"><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3iRpNY9\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">full-fat coconut milk</a></span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">2</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">tablespoons</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">cilantro</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">roughly chopped</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">¼</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">cup</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">chives</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">roughly chopped</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">2</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">tablespoons</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">freshly squeezed lime juice</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">½</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">teaspoon</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">kosher salt</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">¼</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">teaspoon</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">freshly ground black pepper</span></li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n   <div class=\"wprm-unit-conversion-container wprm-unit-conversion-container-links wprm-block-text-normal\" style=\"\">\n    <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/?p=7718#\" role=\"button\" class=\"wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active\" data-system=\"1\" data-recipe=\"7720\" style=\"\" aria-label=\"Change unit system to US Customary\">US Customary</a> – \n    <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/?p=7718#\" role=\"button\" class=\"wprm-unit-conversion\" data-system=\"2\" data-recipe=\"7720\" style=\"\" aria-label=\"Change unit system to Metric\">Metric</a>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Instructions</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-group\">\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions\">\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7720-step-0-0\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       In a bowl, stir together the oil, oregano, garlic, and lime zest.&nbsp;Toss in the shrimp.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7720-step-0-1\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Mix well, making sure that the shrimp is evenly covered. Refrigerate for 30 minutes or up to 2 hours. (No time to marinate the shrimp? It’ll still taste good!)\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7720-step-0-2\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Combine the diced white onion and minced cilantro in a small bowl, and refrigerate until ready to serve.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7720-step-0-3\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Next, make the Avocado Crema. (Psst! This is the same Avocado Crema that I make for my \n       <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/20170613sheet-pan-chicken-fajitas-avocado-crema\">Sheet Pan Chicken Fajitas</a>!) Cut the avocado in half lengthwise and remove the seed. Scoop the flesh into a food processor or blender. Add the coconut milk, cilantro, chives, lime juice, salt, and pepper.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7720-step-0-4\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Blitz until smooth. Add some water to thin out the sauce if desired.Taste and adjust the seasoning as needed with salt, pepper, or more lime juice. You can refrigerate the crema in a container for up to 2 days.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7720-step-0-5\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       When you’re ready to cook the shrimp, set the oven to 400°F with the rack in the middle position. Toss the shrimp with the salt and black pepper. Then, arrange the shrimp in a single layer on a parchment-lined baking sheet.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7720-step-0-6\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Pop it in the oven.&nbsp;Roast for 6 to 8 minutes or until the shrimp is cooked through.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7720-step-0-7\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Arrange the shrimp on lettuce leaves (a.k.a. nature’s tortillas!) and top with the diced onion and cilantro mixture and lime wedges.&nbsp;Drizzle or squirt avocado crema on the tacos.\n      </div></li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div id=\"wprm-recipe-video-container-7720\" class=\"wprm-recipe-video-container\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-video-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Video</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-video\"> \n    <div class=\"adthrive-video-player in-post\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"https://schema.org/VideoObject\" data-video-id=\"L1M4qLZa\" data-player-type=\"default\" override-embed=\"default\"> \n     <meta itemprop=\"uploadDate\" content=\"2020-06-18T00:46:12.000Z\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"name\" content=\"Paleo Shrimp Tacos (Whole30, Keto)\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"description\" content=\"These Paleo Shrimp Tacos are a simple and delicious weeknight supper! Plus, you can make this keto and Whole30 recipe in a flash!\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"thumbnailUrl\" content=\"https://content.jwplatform.com/thumbs/L1M4qLZa-720.jpg\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"contentUrl\" content=\"https://content.jwplatform.com/videos/L1M4qLZa.mp4\" /> \n    </div> \n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-notes-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-notes-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Notes</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-notes\">\n    <span style=\"display: block;\"><strong>How To Cook On A Traeger Grill</strong></span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\">\n     <!-- /wp:heading -->\n     <!-- wp:paragraph --></span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\">If you’ve got a Traeger grill, you can use it like an outdoor oven and throw the sheet pan of marinated shrimp in it. I’ve learned through some trial and error that my oven recipes can cook in a Traeger, but you need to increase the temperature by about 25°F (i.e. for this recipe, cook in the Traeger at 425°F for 6 to 8 minutes or until just cooked through).</span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\">\n     <!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n     <!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --></span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\"><strong>How To Cook On A Gas Grill</strong></span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\">\n     <!-- /wp:heading -->\n     <!-- wp:paragraph --></span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\">Got a gas grill? Soak some bamboo skewers in water for 30 minutes. Grab a skewer and thread about 6 to 8 shrimp on it. &nbsp;Repeat the process until all the shrimp are skewered.&nbsp;</span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\">Crank the burners on the gas grill to high, cover, and heat until super hot. Then, scrape the grates clean and oil with avocado oil. Place the skewers on the grill and cook covered for 3 to 4 minutes, before flipping and cooking for 2 to 3 more minutes or until pink and just cooked through.</span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\">\n     <!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n     <!-- wp:heading --></span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\"><strong>Air Fryer Cooking Instructions</strong></span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\">\n     <!-- /wp:heading -->\n     <!-- wp:paragraph --></span>\n    <div class=\"wprm-spacer\"></div> \n    <span style=\"display: block;\">Heat the air fryer to 400°F and place the shrimp in a single layer in the cooking basket. Air-fry for 5 to 7 minutes or until pink and just cooked through. You may need to cook the shrimp in batches if the basket is small.</span>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-nutrition-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left There is a red banner on the photo that says paleo, Whole30, and gluten-free.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-2-800.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-2-800-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-2-800-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-2-800-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>A Classic Nom Nom Paleo Recipe!</h2> \n<p>My Spicy Tuna Cakes recipe is definitely one of the most popular recipes from our&nbsp;<a href=\"https://amzn.to/3fI9TOE\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">first&nbsp;cookbook</a> and <a href=\"https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/nom-nom-paleo/id507051584?mt=8&amp;ign-mpt=uo%3D4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">app</a>. In fact, I decided to post it here on the blog so more people could make them! I make these portable savory cakes about once a month ’cause I aways have the humble ingredients on hand.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8340 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa29ax.jpg\" alt=\"Two paleo spicy tuna cakes on a plate.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa29ax.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa29ax-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa29ax-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>What do they taste like?</h2> \n<p>You may not normally associate canned fish with sweet potatoes and jalapeño peppers, but trust me on this one: they’re tender and subtly sweet, with a wickedly peppery bite that sneaks up on you. The heat levels can be adjusted to your taste; amp it up by subbing serrano peppers in place of jalapeño, or turn it down by cutting down on the red pepper flakes. Serve these spicy cakes for breakfast, lunch, or dinner—or whip up an extra-big batch for your next dinner party!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8337 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa17a.jpg\" alt=\"Someone flattening the spicy tuna cake mixture into a muffin pan with the back of a spoon.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa17a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa17a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa17a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>How do you keep the tuna cakes from sticking?</h2> \n<p>One of the most frequent questions I get about this recipe is how to keep the tuna cakes from sticking to the muffin pan. In the directions, I tell you to grease the muffin tin with melted ghee—take this step seriously! Don’t skimp on fat because it’ll make the tuna cakes slide out easier. If the tuna cakes are still stuck, use a small silicone spatula to scrape around and under the cakes to coax them out.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-14827\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/800-01-Pumpkin-Muffins.jpg\" alt=\"A person is adding parchment muffin liners to a muffin tin.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/800-01-Pumpkin-Muffins.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/800-01-Pumpkin-Muffins-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/800-01-Pumpkin-Muffins-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>These days, I skip the greasing part and place parchment muffin liners in the pan because it makes clean-up a breeze! (p.s. Many Nomsters have told me that silicone muffin pans are a great non-stick alternative, too!)</p> \n<h2>What other protein can you use?</h2> \n<p>These savory cakes are totally adaptable and you can use a myriad of canned or leftover cooked seafood. Some of my favorite varieties include cakes made with cooked crab, canned salmon, and boneless/skinless sardines. It’s a fantastic and inexpensive way to get more healthy seafood in your diet!</p> \n<h2>Can you make them ahead and freeze them?</h2> \n<p>These Spicy Tuna Cakes can be stored&nbsp;in the fridge in an air-tight container for up to four days or frozen for up to 3 months. If you have frozen tuna cakes, simply thaw them overnight in the refrigerator.</p> \n<h2>How do you reheat them?</h2> \n<p>When you’re ready to eat your leftovers, skillet-fry the tuna cakes in some melted fat over medium heat. Crisp the edges, and you’re good to go. Don’t reheat them in the microwave unless you want to piss off your family members or co-workers with the fishy smell. The leftover spicy tuna cakes taste great straight from the fridge, so no need to make enemies!</p> \n<h2>Time to make Spicy Tuna Cakes!</h2> \n<p><em>Makes 12</em></p> \n<p>\n <!-- more --></p> \n<p><b>Ingredients:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li>3 tablespoons melted <a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0032RPLSY?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creativeASIN=B0032RPLSY&amp;linkCode=xm2&amp;tag=f05f-20\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">ghee</a>, divided</li> \n <li>10 ounces <a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B004AHDV5A?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creativeASIN=B004AHDV5A&amp;linkCode=xm2&amp;tag=f05f-20\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">canned albacore tuna packed in water</a>, drained</li> \n <li>3 scallions, thinly sliced (about&nbsp;⅓ cup)</li> \n <li>2 tablespoons finely minced fresh cilantro</li> \n <li>1⅓ cup mashed&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/1667354361/baked-yamssweet-potatoes\">baked sweet potato</a></li> \n <li>finely grated zest from&nbsp;½ medium lemon</li> \n <li>1 tablespoon minced jalapeño pepper</li> \n <li>2 large eggs</li> \n <li>½ teaspoon red pepper flakes</li> \n <li>Kosher salt</li> \n <li>Freshly ground black pepper</li> \n <li>3 medium lemons, cut into wedges (optional)</li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Equipment:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2aJPZpG\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Silicone brush</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2aLYopw\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">12-cup muffin tin</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2ap69F5\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Parchment muffin liners</a> (optional)</li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2aLYT2T\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Large bowl</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2afZaIV\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Kitchen knife</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2aHxQr3\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Cutting board</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2ajmNjM\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Microplane</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2afYTFU\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Measuring spoons</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2aphbo5\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Measuring cups</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"http://amzn.to/2afZes6\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">Large disher</a></li> \n</ul> \n<p><b>Method:</b></p> \n<p>Preheat the oven to 350°F, and use a brush to grease a <a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B000F5K3J8?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creativeASIN=B000F5K3J8&amp;linkCode=xm2&amp;tag=f05f-20\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">12-cup regular sized muffin tin</a> with one tablespoon of melted ghee. (Or skip this part and just line the tin with <a href=\"http://amzn.to/2ap69F5\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">parchment muffin liners</a>!)</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8343 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC16.jpg\" alt=\"Brushing grease in the muffin tins.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC16.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC16-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC16-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>In a large bowl, mix together the tuna, scallions, and cilantro.&nbsp;Add the mashed sweet potato to the tuna mixture, and gently combine.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8335 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakes4.jpg\" alt=\"The ingredients for spicy tuna cakes mixed together in a bowl.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakes4.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakes4-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakes4-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Then, mix in the lemon zest, jalapeño, the remaining two tablespoons of ghee, eggs, and red pepper flakes.&nbsp;Season with salt and pepper to taste. I normally use 1½ teaspoons of Diamond Crystal brand kosher salt, but your taste may vary.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8342 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC13b.jpg\" alt=\"A raw egg is added to the spicy tuna cake mixture in a bowl.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC13b.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC13b-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC13b-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>(Not sure if you’ve added enough S&amp;P? Take a small portion and fry up a little pancake to see if the seasoning is right!)</p> \n<p>I use my hands to mix everything together because that way I can make sure that the fish chunks aren’t overly broken up.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8336 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa13a.jpg\" alt=\"Someone mixing together the spicy tuna cake mixture with their hands.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa13a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa13a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa13a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Scoop a&nbsp;¼&nbsp;quarter cup of the mixture into each greased muffin tin cup, and flatten with the back of a spoon.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8341 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaaaSTC17a.jpg\" alt=\"Flattening the spicy tuna cakes into the muffin tin with the back of a spoon.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaaaSTC17a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaaaSTC17a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaaaSTC17a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Bake the tuna cakes for 20-25 minutes or until an inserted toothpick comes out cleanly.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8338 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa23.jpg\" alt=\"Someone checking the doneness of the spicy tuna cakes with a toothpick.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa23.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa23-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesa23-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Transfer the cakes to a wire rack to cool. The easiest way I’ve found to get them out is to put the wire rack on top of the muffin tin…</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8344 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC27.jpg\" alt=\"Someone getting ready to transfer the spicy tuna cakes onto a wire rack to cool.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC27.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC27-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC27-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>…flip everything upside-down, and tap them gently on the counter.&nbsp;<i>Voilà!</i></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-8345 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC27a.jpg\" alt=\"Spicy tuna cakes on a wire rack to cool.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC27a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC27a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC27a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Grab a lemon wedge and squeeze some juice on your tuna cake before you pop it in your mouth. Now go make a mess in your kitchen!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19584\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-800.jpg\" alt=\"A collage of the cooking steps to make Spicy Tuna Cakes, a classic Nom Nom Paleo recipe.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-800.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-800-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-800-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-800-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>[Originally posted on July 10, 2014. Updated with new details and photos on July 19, 2020.]</p> \n<hr /> \n<p><em>Looking for more recipe ideas? Head on over to my&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/recipeindex\">Recipe Index</a>. Not!</a>&nbsp;(Andrews McMeel Publishing 2017)!</em></p> \n<div align=\"center\"></div> \n<hr /> \n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\">&nbsp;PRINTER-FRIENDLY RECIPE CARD</h3> \n<div stroke-linejoin=\"miter\" />\n     </g>\n    </svg></span>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-spacer\" style=\"height: 5px\"></div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-summary wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <span style=\"display: block;\">These portable spicy tuna cakes filled with sweet potato and jalapeño peppers are delicious, tender and Whole30-friendly!</span>\n  </div> \n  <div water</a></span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">drained</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span
