data-recipe=\"7001\" style=\"\" aria-label=\"Change unit system to Metric\">Metric</a>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Instructions</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-group\">\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions\">\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7001-step-0-0\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Preheat the oven to 350°F, and use a brush to grease a \n       <a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B000F5K3J8?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creativeASIN=B000F5K3J8&amp;linkCode=xm2&amp;tag=f05f-20\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">12-cup regular sized muffin tin</a> with one tablespoon of melted ghee. (Or skip this part and just line the tin with \n       <a href=\"http://amzn.to/2ap69F5\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">parchment muffin liners</a>!)\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7001-step-0-1\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       In a large bowl, mix together the tuna, scallions, and cilantro.&nbsp;Add the mashed sweet potato to the tuna mixture, and gently combine.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7001-step-0-2\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Then, mix in the lemon zest, jalapeño, the remaining two tablespoons of ghee, eggs, and red pepper flakes.&nbsp;Season with salt and pepper to taste. I normally use&nbsp;1½&nbsp;teaspoons of Diamond Crystal brand kosher salt, but your taste may vary.&nbsp;(Not sure if you’ve added enough S&amp;P? Take a small portion and fry up a little pancake to see if the seasoning is right!)\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7001-step-0-3\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Use your hands to mix everything together because that way you can make sure that the fish chunks aren’t overly broken up.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7001-step-0-4\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Scoop a&nbsp;¼ cup of the mixture into each greased muffin tin cup&nbsp;and flatten with the back of a spoon.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7001-step-0-5\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Bake the tuna cakes for 20-25 minutes or until an inserted toothpick comes out cleanly.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7001-step-0-6\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Transfer the cakes to a wire rack to cool. The easiest way I’ve found to get them out is to put the wire rack on top of the muffin tin,&nbsp;flip everything upside-down, and tap them gently on the counter.&nbsp;\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-7001-step-0-7\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Grab a lemon wedge and squeeze some juice on your tuna cake before your pop it in your mouth. </span>\n      </div></li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div id=\"wprm-recipe-video-container-7001\" class=\"wprm-recipe-video-container\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-video-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Video</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-video\"> \n    <div class=\"adthrive-video-player in-post\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"https://schema.org/VideoObject\" data-video-id=\"tKDQKO2n\" data-player-type=\"\" override-embed=\"\"> \n     <meta itemprop=\"uploadDate\" content=\"2019-09-14T04:49:24.000Z\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"name\" content=\"Spicy Tuna Cakes\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"description\" content=\"These portable tuna, sweet potato, and jalapeño peppers are delicious and Whole30-friendly! 6b9.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/800SpicyTunaCakesaSTC27a.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn93@2020_5/2020/08/24/23-02-01-342_f0f2b972ce52144e.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-800.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn53@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-01-59-220_4d2214b7253af5f9.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/Spicy-Tuna-Cakes-1-150x150.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn78@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-02-00-267_c0fdeef87bb91a10.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598310085735},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","title":"Matcha Lemonade (Green Tea Arnold Palmer)","link":"https://nomnompaleo.com/?p=19491","description":"<p><i>This refreshing and simple matcha lemonade is the perfect, not-too-sweet, summer drink! You can whip up this green tea&nbsp;Arnold Palmer in minutes without turning on the stove or using special&nbsp;equipment!</i></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19493\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Matcha-Lemonade-800.jpg\" alt=\"A clear glass filled with bright green matcha lemonade. A red banner states that it is refined sugar-free and honey sweetened.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Matcha-Lemonade-800.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Matcha-Lemonade-800-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Matcha-Lemonade-800-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Matcha-Lemonade-800-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Another Iced Matcha Drink!</h2> \n<p>As regular Nomsters know, I’m a big fan of drinking and <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/matcha-mug-cake-paleo-gluten-free\">cooking with matcha</a>, a finely ground powder of specially grown green tea leaves. Although matcha is normally served hot, simply whisked with 175°F water, I prefer the ease of making a cold matcha drink—like <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/2017050920170509cold-matcha-latte\">Cold Matcha Latte</a> or <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/cold-brew-matcha\">Cold Brew Matcha</a>—in the hot summer months.</p> \n<p>Recently, I was craving a matcha Arnold Palmer and realized that I could make one easily by doctoring my <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/cold-brew-matcha\">Cold Brew Matcha</a> recipe!</p> \n<h2><strong>A Green Tea Arnold Palmer!</strong></h2> \n<p>A traditional <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arnold_Palmer_(drink)\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">Arnold Palmer drink</a> is a refreshing non-alcoholic beverage made with three parts unsweetened tea combined with one part lemonade. However, it’s not a quick drink if you don’t already have some brewed tea and lemonade in the fridge.</p> \n<p>When I started making <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/cold-brew-matcha\">Cold Brew Matcha</a>, I learned that you can make a cup of green tea by simply shaking matcha vigorously with cold water. By adding freshly squeezed lemon juice and honey, you can transform it into a mildly sweet Matcha Lemonade in no time!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19497\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2466a.jpg\" alt=\"Someone juicing a lemon with a stainless steel citrus juicer.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2466a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2466a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2466a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>What Matcha Should You Use?</h2> \n<p>My favorite brand and type of matcha for this type of recipe—where you mix matcha with other ingredients besides water—is <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2Z2pnHi\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">this one</a>. You don’t need to break the bank and buy the most expensive matcha available, but find one that is bright green and tastes good to you.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19510\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2485a.jpg\" alt=\"An overhead shot of someone measuring out a spoonful of bright green matcha.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2485a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2485a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2485a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Three Ways to Make It!</h2> \n<p>There are a few simple ways to make this refreshing matcha lemonade. You can use an inexpensive milk frother or small hand whisk to whip it up with minimal effort. However, the easiest method is to dump all the ingredients in a mason jar and shake like mad! All three methods work great and cleanup is a breeze.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19511\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2754a.jpg\" alt=\"A smiling brunette woman in glasses is holding a matcha lemonade with a glass straw.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2754a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2754a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2754a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2754a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Time to make a Matcha Lemonade a.k.a. Green Tea Arnold Palmer!</h2> \n<p><em>Serves 1</em></p> \n<p><strong>Ingredients:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>1 teaspoon matcha (I like <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3e0wqnX\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">this one</a>.)</li> \n <li>1 tablespoon lemon juice</li> \n <li>1 tablespoon honey or more to taste</li> \n <li>1 cup cold water</li> \n <li>Ice cubes</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Equipment:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>All of my recommended kitchen tools are listed <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/shop/nomnompaleo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\"><strong>here</strong></a>. The inexpensive milk frother I like is <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2CayxIQ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">this one</a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<h2>There are three ways to make this refreshing drink!</h2> \n<h3><strong>Using A Small Hand Whisk:</strong></h3> \n<p>Combine the matcha and lemon juice in a measuring cup…</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19502\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2820b.jpg\" alt=\"Adding a spoonful of matcha and lemon juice into a liquid measuring cup.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2820b.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2820b-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2820b-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>…and whisk well until the matcha is in a uniform suspension.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19503\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2860a.jpg\" alt=\"Someone whisking together matcha and lemon juice in a measuring cup.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2860a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2860a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2860a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Whisk in the honey.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19504\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2919a.jpg\" alt=\"Adding a spoonful of honey to a liquid measuring cup with a small hand whisk inside.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2919a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2919a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2919a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Once the honey is incorporated, mix in the cold water.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19505\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2939a.jpg\" alt=\"Pouring water into the matcha mixture in the liquid measuring cup.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2939a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2939a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2939a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Pour over ice and enjoy!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19506\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2704b.jpg\" alt=\"Pouring the matcha lemonade (Green Tea Arnold Palmer) in a glass filled with ice.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2704b.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2704b-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2704b-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h3>Using A Milk Frother:</h3> \n<p>Add the matcha, lemon juice, honey, and water to a liquid measuring cup and use a milk frother to blitz everything into an emerald green liquid.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19507\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2564a.jpg\" alt=\"Blending a matcha lemonade with a milk frother\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2564a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2564a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2564a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h3>Using A Mason Jar:</h3> \n<p>Measure all the ingredients and add them into a pint-sized mason jar. Screw on the lid tightly and shake like mad until the matcha is evenly dispersed!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19508\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2666a.jpg\" alt=\"Shaking the matcha lemonade (green tea Arnold Palmer) in a mason jar.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2666a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2666a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2666a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Whichever method you choose will result in an icy delight!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19509\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2799a-1.jpg\" alt=\"A woman in glasses is holding up a glass of matcha lemonade\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2799a-1.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2799a-1-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2799a-1-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2799a-1-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<hr /> \n<p><em>Looking for more recipe ideas? https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn86@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-02-01-145_5c838ed27e805656.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2799a-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn10@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-01-59-289_adbb921851c93c0a.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2790a-150x150.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn98@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-02-00-397_fb33dfa9b5e1759c.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2820b-300x200.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn6@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-02-01-306_40c0481fe078a845.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2919a-300x200.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn30@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-02-00-114_1b38e45a3fe67935.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2704b-300x200.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn34@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-02-00-308_4229791f616d8107.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2564a-300x200.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn97@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-02-02-895_cbf593796fdb810d.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800-Matcha-Lemonade-aaDSC_2666a-300x200.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn50@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-02-01-556_1e44ec3c53f8ddb1.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598310085735},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","title":"Watercress Salad With Peaches and Prosciutto (Whole30, Paleo)","link":"https://nomnompaleo.com/2014/07/17/watercress-with-seared-prosciutto-peaches/","description":"<p><em>Heads up: A 10-minute Whole30 summer meal comin’ your way: Watercress Salad with Peaches and Prosciutto! This fresh and healthy salad is summer on a&nbsp;</em><i>plate!</i></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-19474 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Watercress-with-Seared-Prosciutto-and-Peaches-800.jpg\" alt=\"A closeup shot of a white plate topped with watercress salad with prosciutto-wrapped seared peaches and pistachios. There is a red banner at the bottom that lists that this recipe is paleo, Whole30, and gluten-free.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Watercress-with-Seared-Prosciutto-and-Peaches-800.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Watercress-with-Seared-Prosciutto-and-Peaches-800-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Watercress-with-Seared-Prosciutto-and-Peaches-800-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Watercress-with-Seared-Prosciutto-and-Peaches-800-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>A Restaurant Favorite At Home!</h2> \n<p>Prosciutto-wrapped peaches on a bed of bitter greens is a classic Italian starter that I used to order every time I spotted it on a summer menu…’til&nbsp;it finally dawned on me that this dead-simple recipe can be made at home for pennies on the dollar. Yeah, I can be dense sometimes. It took this old dog a decade to learn this peachy new trick, but hey: better late than never, right?</p> \n<p>Once ripe peaches made their first appearance of the year at the local farmers’ market, I started making this savory, sweet, and assertive summer salad on a regular basis. Can you blame me? I mean, the hardest part is just wrapping prosciutto around peach slices!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-10338 size-large\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3672WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-800x1200.jpg\" alt=\"A close-up shot of a slice of peach wrapped with a thin slice of prosciutto.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3672WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3672WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3672WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3672WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-750x1125.jpg 750w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3672WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x900.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Seared Peaches are better than Grilled Peaches!</h2> \n<p>Most recipes call for grilling the porky peaches, but I’ve found that searing ’em in a skillet is a much easier and faster method. In fact, it takes longer to fire up the barbecue than it does to prepare&nbsp;<em>and</em> eat this gorgeous hot-weather salad using a skillet.</p> \n<h2>Watercress Salad!</h2> \n<p>In my version of this classic dish, I also replaced the usual bed of arugula with watercress. Both types of greens add a pleasing bitter bite to this salad, but watercress is the <a href=\"http://www.cdc.gov/pcd/issues/2014/13_0390.htm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">new Queen Bee of the vegetable aisle</a>&nbsp;(that’s right: move over, kale),&nbsp;and I’ve been doing my darnedest to incorporate this nutrient-packed powerhouse into my diet. Plus, the warm peaches wilt the watercress slightly, making each mouthful &nbsp;a kaleidoscope of flavors and textures.</p> \n<h2>What can you use in place of prosciutto?</h2> \n<p>If you can’t find prosciutto at the market, you can sear the peaches without wrapping them with anything. Bacon slices are too thick and won’t crisp up before the peaches get overcooked. I prefer to fry up chopped up bacon bits and add them to the salad if I still want some salty porky goodness. Don’t eat pork? Crumble on some crispy <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/chicken-cracklings\">Chicken Cracklings</a>!</p> \n<h2>Let’s make Watercress Salad With Peaches and Prosciutto!</h2> \n<p>\n <!-- more --></p> \n<p><em>Serves 1 as an entree or 2 as an appetizer</em></p> \n<p><strong>Ingredients:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>2 cups watercress, thin stems and leaves only</li> \n <li>1 ripe (but still firm) peach</li> \n <li>6 thin slices prosciutto (I like La Quercia brand)</li> \n <li>1 teaspoon <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2L243rM\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">ghee</a> or <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2uiEyvu\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">avocado oil</a></li> \n <li>1 tablespoon shelled dry-roasted and salted pistachios</li> \n <li>1 tablespoon <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2zoInox\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">extra virgin olive oil</a></li> \n <li>2 teaspoons aged balsamic vinegar</li> \n <li>Freshly cracked black pepper</li> \n</ul> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-10333 size-large\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3618aWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-800x1200.jpg\" alt=\"Prosciutto, watercress, and a peach sitting on a counter for the Watercress with Seared Prosciutto and Peaches recipe.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3618aWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3618aWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3618aWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3618aWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-750x1125.jpg 750w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3618aWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x900.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p><strong>Equipment:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>All of my recommended kitchen tools are listed <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/shop/nomnompaleo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\"><strong>here</strong></a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Method:</strong></p> \n<p>Grab a big bunch of watercress and pick off the tender leaves and thin stems until you have 2 cups of salad greens. (Reserve the rest to add to soup. Like <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/129592158903/simple-egg-drop-soup\">Simple Egg Drop Soup</a>!)</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-10334 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3623WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg\" alt=\"Watercress sitting in a colander.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3623WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3623WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3623WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x512.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3623WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Wash and spin dry the greens before dumping ’em on a plate.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-10335 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3645WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg\" alt=\"A peach sliced in half sitting on a counter.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3645WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3645WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3645WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x512.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3645WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Slice your peach in half, remove the pit, and divide each half into thirds to get six slices. Wrap a slice of prosciutto around each wedge of fruit.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-10336 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3653WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg\" alt=\"Quartered peaches, a slice of prosciutto, and washed watercress sitting on a cutting board.\" width=\"800\" height=\"534\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3653WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3653WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3653WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x513.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3653WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x401.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>The prosciutto should be coiled flat and tight around the peach slice.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-10337 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3664WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg\" alt=\"A quartered peach wrapped with a thin slice of prosciutto.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3664WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3664WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3664WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x512.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3664WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>While you’re preparing the peaches, heat a skillet or griddle over medium-high heat. Add the ghee or avocado oil, and swirl to coat the pan. When the pan is hot, lay the peaches on one side and cook for about a minute or until browned. Then, flip each wedge over onto its other flat side, and cook for another 30-60 seconds.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-10339 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3689WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg\" alt=\"Prosciutto wrapped peaches searing on a cast iron skillet.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3689WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3689WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3689WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x512.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3689WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>When the peaches are browned on both sides, flip them peach-skin side down. and brown the bottom for 30-60 seconds.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-10340 size-large\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3695WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-800x1200.jpg\" alt=\"A close up of prosciutto-wrapped peached searing on a cast iron skillet.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3695WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3695WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3695WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3695WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-750x1125.jpg 750w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3695WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x900.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Place the hot peaches on the bed of watercress. Chop up the pistachios and sprinkle on top of the salad.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-10332 size-full\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3115WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg\" alt=\"Overhead shot of crushed and chopped pistachios ready for the Watercress with Seared Prosciutto and Peaches.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3115WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3115WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3115WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x512.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaaDSC_3115WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x400.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Add a generous drizzle of extra virgin olive oil and balsamic vinegar to taste, and top with freshly cracked black pepper.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-10342\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaDSC_3730bWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-800x1200.jpg\" alt=\"Watercress With Seared Prosciutto + Peaches by Michelle Tam https://nomnompaleo.com\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaDSC_3730bWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaDSC_3730bWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaDSC_3730bWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaDSC_3730bWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-750x1125.jpg 750w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaDSC_3730bWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-600x900.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>[Originally posted on July 9, 2018. Updated with new details and photos on June 28, 2020.]</p> \n<hr /> \n<p><em>Looking for more recipe ideas? Head on over to my&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/recipeindex\">Recipe Index</a>. href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/foodforhumanscookbook\">Nom Nom Paleo: Food for Humans</a>&nbsp;(Andrews McMeel Publishing 2013) and&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/readyornotcookbook\">Ready or Not!</a>&nbsp;(Andrews McMeel Publishing 2017)!</em></p> \n<hr /> \n<h3 align=\"center\">PRINTER-FRIENDLY RECIPE CARD</h3> \n<div id=\"wprm-recipe-container-10324\" class=\"wprm-recipe-container\" + Peaches by Michelle Tam https://nomnompaleo.com\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/400aaaDSC_3730WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-150x150.jpg 150w, class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Instructions</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-group\">\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions\">\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-10324-step-0-0\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Grab a big bunch of watercress and pick off the tender leaves and thin stems until you have 2 cups of salad greens. (Reserve the rest to add to soup. Like \n       <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/129592158903/simple-egg-drop-soup\">Simple Egg Drop Soup</a>!)&nbsp;Wash and spin dry the greens before dumping ’em on a plate.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-10324-step-0-1\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Slice your peach in half, remove the pit, and divide each half into thirds to get six slices. Wrap a slice of prosciutto around each wedge of fruit.&nbsp;The prosciutto should be coiled flat and tight around the peach slice.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-10324-step-0-2\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       While you’re preparing the peaches, heat a skillet or griddle over medium-high heat. Add the ghee or avocado oil, and swirl to coat the pan. When the pan is hot, lay the peaches on one side and cook for about a minute or until browned. Then, flip each wedge over onto its other flat side, and cook for another 30-60 seconds.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-10324-step-0-3\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       When the peaches are browned on both sides, flip them peach-skin side down. and brown the bottom for 30-60 seconds.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-10324-step-0-4\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Place the hot peaches on the bed of watercress. Chop up the pistachios and sprinkle on top of the salad.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-10324-step-0-5\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Add a generous drizzle of extra virgin olive oil and balsamic vinegar to taste, and top with freshly cracked black pepper.\n      </div></li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div id=\"wprm-recipe-video-container-10324\" class=\"wprm-recipe-video-container\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-video-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Video</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-video\"> \n    <div class=\"adthrive-video-player in-post\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"https://schema.org/VideoObject\" data-video-id=\"mgT1Giz4\" data-player-type=\"default\" override-embed=\"default\"> \n     <meta itemprop=\"uploadDate\" content=\"2020-06-29T03:07:25.000Z\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"name\" content=\"Watercress Salad with Peaches and Prosciutto\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"description\" content=\"Watercress Salad with Peaches and Prosciutto is one of my favorite summertime salads! Peaches.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn98@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-01-59-182_5d703b6e7a235e83.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/800aaDSC_3730bWatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-800x1200.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn89@2020_5/2020/08/24/23-02-01-882_d63eaf7180604c76.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/400aaaDSC_3730WatercressSearedProsciuttoPeaches-150x150.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn98@2020_6/2020/08/24/23-01-59-137_d86bc6a315b01ae4.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598310085736},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","title":"Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bons (Paleo, Vegan, Gluten Free)","link":"https://nomnompaleo.com/2013/07/08/chunky-monkey-ice-cream-bon-bons/","description":"<p><i>Love frozen&nbsp;bananas,&nbsp;chocolate, and toasted nuts? These Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bons are a healthy and delicious dairy-free, paleo, and vegan frozen dessert! Best of all, they’re super simple to make with just a few ingredients that you&nbsp;may already have&nbsp;in your kitchen!</i></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19538\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Chunky-Monkey-Ice-Cream-Bon-Bons-800.jpg\" alt=\"A shot of a parchment lined baking sheet topped with Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bons, a paleo, vegan, and dairy-free treat!\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Chunky-Monkey-Ice-Cream-Bon-Bons-800.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Chunky-Monkey-Ice-Cream-Bon-Bons-800-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Chunky-Monkey-Ice-Cream-Bon-Bons-800-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Chunky-Monkey-Ice-Cream-Bon-Bons-800-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>My Inspirations For This Paleo Dessert!</h2> \n<p>I love shortcuts to deliciousness, especially for paleo dessert recipes! I came up with this simple, bite-sized confection by merging together two of my favorite recipes—The Kitchn’s&nbsp;<a href=\"http://www.thekitchn.com/stepbystep-instructions-for-on-97170\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">One Ingredient Ice Cream</a> and Irvin Lin’s homemade&nbsp;<a href=\"http://www.eatthelove.com/2011/03/wordless-recipe-how-to-make-own-ice-cream-magic-chocolate-hard-shell/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">Magic Shell</a>. Plus, it’s a fantastic way to use up ripe bananas when you’re sick of making my <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/144116008838/strawberry-banana-ice-cream\">Strawberry Banana Ice Cream</a>!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19544\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7437a.jpg\" alt=\"A closeup shot of a Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bon, a healthy paleo dessert.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7437a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7437a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7437a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7437a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Timing is key!</h2> \n<p>The steps for this recipe are easy, but timing is key. You <i>must</i> wait for the “ice cream” to freeze completely (twice!) before proceeding, and then you gotta work <i>fast</i>. Otherwise, you’ll end up with melty brown lumps.</p> \n<h2>My Favorite Dark Chocolate</h2> \n<p>Because this recipe only uses six ingredients, quality matters—especially when you’re choosing the dark chocolate for the coating. I normally chop up dark chocolate bars (ranging from 70% to 85% cacao) that I would snack on, including <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2OlhgiR\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Green &amp; Black Organic Dark Chocolate</a> and <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2ZsCOk5\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Alter Eco</a> brands. If you’re too lazy to chop up the chocolate, you can use <a href=\"https://amzn.to/390FFUw\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Hu Gems</a> or <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2Wg0ztw\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Pascha Chocolate Chips</a>.</p> \n<h2>Time to make Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bons!</h2> \n<p><em>Makes 24 Bon Bons</em></p> \n<p><b>Ingredients:</b></p> \n<ul> \n <li>3 medium ripe bananas, frozen and cut into 1-inch pieces</li> \n <li>1 teaspoon vanilla extract</li> \n <li>7 ounces dark chocolate (70% cacao or higher), finely chopped</li> \n <li>¼ cup coconut oil</li> \n <li>⅛ teaspoon Diamond Crystal kosher salt</li> \n <li>3 tablespoons toasted slivered almonds or toasted chopped walnuts (Chunky Monkey ice cream typically contains walnuts, but I prefer almonds)</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Equipment:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>All of my recommended kitchen tools are listed <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/shop/nomnompaleo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\"><strong>here</strong></a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>\n <!-- more --></p> \n<p><b>Method:</b></p> \n<p>First things first: you gotta make your banana ice cream. Mine isn’t quite one-ingredient—I use two—but it’s drop-dead simple nonetheless, and doesn’t require an ice cream maker. (I have a similar recipe for a 2-minute Strawberry Banana Ice Cream in&nbsp;<a href=\"https://amzn.to/2MXDUfc\" rel=\"nofollow sponsored\">my first cookbook</a>!)</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19548\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7166a.jpg\" alt=\"Three frozen bananas and a bottle of vanilla extract are on a wooden cutting board.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7166a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7166a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7166a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7166a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Toss the frozen banana chunks and vanilla into a blender or food processor…</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19549\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7172a.jpg\" alt=\"An overhead shot of frozen banana slices in an open food processor.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7172a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7172a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7172a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>…and blitz until smooth and creamy.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19550\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7202a.jpg\" alt=\"A food processor filled with creamy banana ice cream.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7202a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7202a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7202a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7202a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Transfer the ice cream to an airtight container and freeze until solid but scoopable (about 2 hours).</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19551\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7211a.jpg\" alt=\"Transferring vegan banana ice cream to a class container with a blue silicone spatula.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7211a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7211a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7211a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7211a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>I know you’re itching to complete the recipe, but it’ll take some time for the ice cream to harden. Go for a long, leisurely walk to the park, and avoid opening the freezer every 20 minutes to check on your ice cream. You’ll drive yourself crazy.</p> \n<p>Once your ice cream has firmed up, use a small disher to scoop it into teaspoon-sized balls. Place them on a parchment lined tray.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19552\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7281a.jpg\" alt=\"Using a small dishes to transfer vegan banana ice cream scoops on a parchment lined rimmed baking sheet.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7281a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7281a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7281a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Work quickly—you don’t want your ice cream to melt.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19553\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7297a.jpg\" alt=\"Closeup of the paleo banana ice cream scoops on a parchment lined baking sheet.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7297a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7297a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7297a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Place the tray in the freezer and chill until the scoops are solid. <i>Really</i> solid. If you can stand the wait, I recommend letting them sit overnight in the freezer. Trust me on this.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19554\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7314a.jpg\" alt=\"A side shot of a rimmed baking sheet filled with scoops of dairy-free banana ice cream.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7314a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7314a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7314a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7314a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>When you’re ready to assemble the bon bons, throw the chocolate, coconut oil, and salt in a heat-proof bowl. Place the bowl over a saucepan filled with simmering water, making sure the water does not come in contact with the bottom of the bowl.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19555\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7330a.jpg\" alt=\"Sliced chocolate and coconut oil are being mixed in a glass bowl.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7330a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7330a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7330a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Stir the chocolate mixture constantly until completely melted.&nbsp;(Alternatively, you can just nuke the chocolate mixture in 30 second increments in a microwave until melted.)</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19556\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7365a.jpg\" alt=\"A blue silicone spatula is mixing a bowl of melted chocolate.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7365a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7365a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7365a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7365a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Take the chocolate off the heat and let it cool to room temperature. It should stay liquid for several hours as long as your house is above&nbsp;70°F. If your house is colder than that, your air conditioning is on too high.</p> \n<p>Remove the solid banana ice cream scoops out of the freezer. Stab a skewer into the flat bottom of an ice cream ball…</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19557\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7377a.jpg\" alt=\"A banana ice cream scoop on a skewer is being dipped in melted chocolate to make Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bons.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7377a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7377a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7377a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" />…and quickly dip it in the melted chocolate…</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19558\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7387a.jpg\" alt=\"A banana ice cream scoop is covered in melted chocolate.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7387a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7387a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7387a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>…or just spoon it on.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19559\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7418a.jpg\" alt=\"Spooning melted chocolate over a small scoop of banana ice cream to make Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bons.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7418a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7418a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7418a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7418a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Before the chocolate shell hardens, sprinkle on the chopped nuts.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19560\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7408a.jpg\" alt=\"Someone adding slivered almonds to a Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bon.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7408a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7408a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7408a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Don’t dawdle. The “ice cream” can melt quickly, and the chocolate magic shell hardens fast, so the most efficient way to coat these treats is to get the whole family involved. Give everyone a skewer—you can eat as you make ‘em.</p> \n<p>Keep the skewers on if you want to enjoy these treats as a Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Pop (just cut off the pointy ends so you don’t stab yourselves)…</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19561\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7403a.jpg\" alt=\"Someone in a black shirt holding a Chunky Monkey ice Cream Bon Bon on a wooden skewer.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7403a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7403a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7403a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7403a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>…or you can keep your bon bons in an airtight container in the freezer for up to a couple of months.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19543\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7473a.jpg\" alt=\"A closeup of a tray of Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bons, a paleo and vegan dessert with banana ice cream topped with a chocolate shell and toasted almonds.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7473a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7473a-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7473a-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7473a-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Now go make your little monkeys happy!</p> \n<p>[Originally posted on July 8, 2013. Updated with new details and photos on July 13, 2020.]</p> \n<hr /> \n<p><em>Looking for more recipe ideas? Head on over to my&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/recipeindex\">Recipe Index</a>. wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Ingredients</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-group\">\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredients\">\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">3</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">medium ripe bananas</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">frozen and cut into 1-inch pieces</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">1</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">teaspoon</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">vanilla extract</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">7</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">ounces</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">dark chocolate</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">70% cacao or higher, finely chopped</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">¼</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">cup</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">coconut oil</span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">⅛</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">teaspoon</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\"><a href=\"https://amzn.to/2t4imEX\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">Diamond Crystal kosher salt&nbsp;</a></span></li>\n     <li class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient\" style=\"list-style-type: disc;\"><span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount\">3</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit\">tablespoons</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-name\">toasted slivered almonds</span> <span class=\"wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded\">or toasted chopped walnuts </span></li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n   <div class=\"wprm-unit-conversion-container wprm-unit-conversion-container-links wprm-block-text-normal\" style=\"\">\n    <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/2013/07/08/chunky-monkey-ice-cream-bon-bons/#\" role=\"button\" class=\"wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active\" data-system=\"1\" data-recipe=\"5737\" style=\"\" aria-label=\"Change unit system to US Customary\">US Customary</a> - \n    <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/2013/07/08/chunky-monkey-ice-cream-bon-bons/#\" role=\"button\" class=\"wprm-unit-conversion\" data-system=\"2\" data-recipe=\"5737\" style=\"\" aria-label=\"Change unit system to Metric\">Metric</a>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Instructions</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-group\">\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions\">\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-0\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">First things first: you gotta make your banana ice cream.&nbsp;Toss the frozen banana chunks and vanilla into a blender or food processor and blitz until smooth and creamy.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-1\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Transfer the ice cream to an airtight container and freeze until solid but scoopable (about 2 hours).\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-2\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Once your ice cream has firmed up, use a small disher to scoop it into teaspoon-sized balls. Place them on a parchment lined tray. (Work quickly—you don’t want your ice cream to melt.)\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-3\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Place the tray in the freezer and chill until the scoops are solid. I recommend letting them sit overnight in the freezer.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-4\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       When you’re ready to finish assembling the bon bons, throw the chocolate, coconut oil, and salt in a heat-proof bowl and place the bowl over a pot of simmering water. (This is what you do if you don’t have a double boiler.)&nbsp;Make sure the water does not touch the bottom of the bowl. Stir the chocolate mixture constantly until completely melted.&nbsp;\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-5\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Alternatively, if you prefer using a microwave oven, you can just nuke the chocolate mixture in 30 second increments until melted.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-6\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Take the chocolate off the heat and let it cool to room temperature. It should stay liquid for several hours as long as your house is above&nbsp;70°F. If your house is colder than that, your air conditioning is on too high.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-7\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Remove the solid scoops out of the freezer. Stab a skewer into the flat bottom of an ice cream ball, and quickly dip it in the melted chocolate&nbsp;or just spoon it on.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-8\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       Before the chocolate shell hardens, sprinkle on the chopped almonds.&nbsp;Don’t dawdle. The “ice cream” can melt quickly, and the chocolate magic shell hardens fast, so the most efficient way to coat these treats is to get the whole family involved. Give everyone a skewer—you can eat as you make ‘em.\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-5737-step-0-9\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">You can store the Bon Bons in a sealed container in the freezer for up to 3 months.</span>\n      </div></li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div id=\"wprm-recipe-video-container-5737\" class=\"wprm-recipe-video-container\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-video-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Video</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-video\"> \n    <div class=\"adthrive-video-player in-post\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"https://schema.org/VideoObject\" data-video-id=\"5E8RA5tI\" data-player-type=\"default\" override-embed=\"default\"> \n     <meta itemprop=\"uploadDate\" content=\"2020-07-13T21:58:42.000Z\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"name\" content=\"Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bons (Paleo, Vegan, Gluten Free)\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"description\" content=\"These Chunky Monkey Ice Cream Bon Bons are a healthy and delicious dairy-free, paleo, and vegan frozen dessert! Best of all, they’re super simple to make!\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"thumbnailUrl\" content=\"https://content.jwplatform.com/thumbs/5E8RA5tI-720.jpg\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"contentUrl\" content=\"https://content.jwplatform.com/videos/5E8RA5tI.mp4\" /> \n    </div> \n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-notes-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-notes-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Notes</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-notes\">\n    <span style=\"display: block;\">The steps are easy, but timing is key. You <i>must</i> wait for the “ice cream” to freeze completely (twice!) before proceeding, and then you gotta work <i>fast</i>. Otherwise, you’ll end up with melty brown lumps.</span>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-nutrition-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn9@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-01-59-217_94641e6bf06457ed.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7377a.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn66@2020_4/2020/08/24/23-02-02-631_2ea418b91e16b29c.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7387a.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn61@2020_4/2020/08/24/23-02-00-946_9fe55b6e406adc68.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7418a.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn22@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-02-01-433_c8cf27a3e4e3794c.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7408a.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn37@2020_4/2020/08/24/23-02-01-540_7ac158038be2f3fd.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7403a.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn77@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-02-01-766_28ed3294cb1a2d51.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7473a.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn49@2020_5/2020/08/24/23-02-00-302_d01f35dbdf67bc39.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/800-Chunky-Monkey-aaDSC_7437a-150x150.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn54@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-02-01-617_e39b0b0771741c4f.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598310085735},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","title":"St. Paul Sandwich (Paleo, Low Carb, Gluten Free)","link":"https://nomnompaleo.com/?p=19640","description":"<p><i>This St. Paul Sandwich is a paleo, low carb, and gluten-free version of the midwestern Chinese-American classic! You can assemble this sandwich in minutes if you already have some Egg Foo Young patties in the fridge!</i></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19643\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/St.-Paul-Sandwich-800.jpg\" alt=\"Someone holding a paleo and gluten-free St. Paul Sandwich. \" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/St.-Paul-Sandwich-800.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/St.-Paul-Sandwich-800-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/St.-Paul-Sandwich-800-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/St.-Paul-Sandwich-800-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>This dish represents me as a sandwich—an umami-packed, paleo-friendly Chinese American leftover makeover!</p> \n<h2>What is a St. Paul Sandwich?</h2> \n<p>A St. Paul sandwich is a midwestern Chinese-American classic: golden-brown egg foo young patties and pickles tucked in-between two pieces of white bread slathered with mayonnaise. Its origins can be traced back to Steven Yuen, the former owner of Park Chop Suey in Lafayette Square near downtown St. Louis, Missouri. Yes, you heard that right: ST. LOUIS. Although this sandwich first gained popularity in St. Louis, the sandwich is allegedly named after Yuen’s hometown of St. Paul, Minnesota!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19651\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3439.jpg\" alt=\"Someone holding two halves of a St. Paul sandwich with gluten-free and paleo-friendly ingredients.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3439.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3439-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3439-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>How is this sandwich Paleo?</h2> \n<p>In this healthier St. Paul sandwich, I’ve cut out the grains in the bread and egg patties, and added paleo-friendly condiments like <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/quick-pickled-red-onions-paleo-whole30-vegan\">Quick Pickled Red Onions</a> and a spicy sriracha mayonnaise to amp up the flavors!</p> \n<h2>Leftover Makeover!</h2> \n<p>I love leftover makeovers because you can easily and quickly transform last night’s meal into something new and exciting. St. Paul sandwiches are one of the best examples of a leftover makeover—two times over!</p> \n<p>My <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/5568966009/egg-foo-young-ish-spinach-egg-ham-coconut\">Egg Foo Young recipe</a> is already a leftover makeover because you can fill the egg-y patties with leftover protein and vegetables. The next day, you can tuck leftover Egg Foo Young patties into these tasty sandwiches! Voilà!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19652\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3373.jpg\" alt=\"Adding quick pickled onions on a paleo and gluten-free St. Paul sandwich.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3373.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3373-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3373-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>I always make a double-batch of <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/5568966009/egg-foo-young-ish-spinach-egg-ham-coconut\">Egg Foo Young</a> patties so I can use the leftovers to make St. Paul Sandwiches. When you’re hangry, you can assemble one in just a few minutes if you have all the ingredients on hand!</p> \n<h2>What Type of Paleo Bread Can You Use?</h2> \n<p>Luckily, paleo-friendly grain-free bread is not so hard to find these days! There are lots of great paleo sandwich bread recipes online, including <a href=\"https://againstallgrain.com/2012/05/21/grain-free-white-bread-paleo-and-scd/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">this one by Danielle Walker</a>. You can also buy a <a href=\"http://www.legitbreadcompany.com/purchase/blonde-legit-bread-mix\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">terrific paleo sandwich bread mix from Legit Bread Company</a>. Too lazy to bake? You can buy fabulous paleo-and keto-friendly loaves from Misfits Bakehouse! They ship nationwide and you can order them <a href=\"https://www.misfits.kitchen\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">here</a>.</p> \n<h2>Guinness World Records Title!</h2> \n<p>On August 6, 2020, I helped set a Guinness Worlds Record title with this sandwich! I joined Al Roker alongside chefs from around the country in this year’s <a href=\"https://www.today.com/food/al-roker-60-chefs-set-guinness-world-record-title-during-t188743\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\">Rokerthon: Al’s Great American Sandwich Relay</a> to break a new Guinness World Records record for the most sandwiches consecutively assembled live!</p> \n<p>You can watch the record setting sandwich relay by clicking <a href=\"https://www.today.com/video/rokerthon-2020-watch-the-entire-great-american-sandwich-relay-89654853730\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"false noopener noreferrer\"><strong>here</strong></a>. Skip to the 2:00:40 mark to see me assembling my St. Paul sandwich!</p> \n<h2>Time to Make St. Paul Sandwiches!</h2> \n<p><em>Makes 4 sandwiches</em></p> \n<p><strong>Ingredients:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>8 <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/5568966009/egg-foo-young-ish-spinach-egg-ham-coconut\">Egg Foo Young</a> patties</li> \n <li><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">½ </span> batch <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/quick-pickled-red-onions-paleo-whole30-vegan\">Quick Pickled Red Onions</a></li> \n <li>¼ cup <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/3440774534/paleo-mayonnaise\">Paleo mayonnaise</a> (store-bought is fine!)</li> \n <li>¼ cup <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/53690118029/whole30-sriracha\">Whole30 Sriracha</a></li> \n <li>8 slices Paleo grain-free bread (see note above for recommendations)</li> \n <li>8 thin tomato slices</li> \n <li>4 leaves Romaine or butter lettuce</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Equipment:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>All of my recommended kitchen tools are listed <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/shop/nomnompaleo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\"><strong>here</strong></a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Method:</strong></p> \n<p>Go grab some&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/5568966009/egg-foo-young-ish-spinach-egg-ham-coconut\">Egg Foo Young</a> patties and your jar of <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/quick-pickled-red-onions-paleo-whole30-vegan\">Quick Pickled Red Onions</a>! You can heat the patties in a toaster oven or air fryer at 325°F for 5 minutes or until warmed through. (You can also assemble the sandwiches with cold Egg Foo Young, too!)</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-7690\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800eggfooyoungaaaDSC_3228-1.jpg\" alt=\"Four paleo egg foo young patties on a white plate.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800eggfooyoungaaaDSC_3228-1.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800eggfooyoungaaaDSC_3228-1-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800eggfooyoungaaaDSC_3228-1-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>In a small bowl, whisk together the mayonnaise and sriracha and slather the sriracha mayonnaise on one side of each piece of bread.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19647\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3329.jpg\" alt=\"A knife is spreading sriracha mayonnaise on a slice of gluten-free and paleo sandwich bread.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3329.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3329-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3329-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Pile each sandwich with two paleo <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/5568966009/egg-foo-young-ish-spinach-egg-ham-coconut\">Egg Foo Young patties</a>, two tomato slices, a handful of <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/quick-pickled-red-onions-paleo-whole30-vegan\">Quick Pickled Red Onions</a>, and a lettuce leaf.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19648\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3411.jpg\" alt=\"Adding a piece of lettuce on a paleo St. Paul sandwich.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3411.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3411-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3411-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Top the remaining pieces of bread on top of the four sandwiches.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19649\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3421.jpg\" alt=\"Two hands topping a paleo and gluten free St. Paul sandwich with a slice of grain-free bread.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3421.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3421-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3421-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Slice each St. Paul sandwich in half and enjoy!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19650\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3504-1.jpg\" alt=\"A closeup shot of someone holding a paleo St. Paul sandwich that has been sliced in half.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3504-1.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3504-1-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3504-1-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3504-1-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<hr /> \n<p><em>Looking for more recipe ideas? Head on over to my&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/recipeindex\">Recipe Index</a>. You’ll also find exclusive recipes on&nbsp;<a href=\"https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/nom-nom-paleo/id507051584?mt=8&amp;ign-mpt=uo%3D4\">my iPhone and iPad app,</a>&nbsp;and in my cookbooks,&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/foodforhumanscookbook\">Nom Nom Paleo: Food for Humans</a>&nbsp;(Andrews McMeel Publishing 2013) and&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/readyornotcookbook\">Ready or Not!</a>&nbsp;(Andrews McMeel Publishing 2017)!</em></p> \n<hr /> \n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\">&nbsp;PRINTER-FRIENDLY RECIPE CARD</h3> \n<div id=\"wprm-recipe-container-19654\" class=\"wprm-recipe-container\" data-recipe-id=\"19654\">\n <div class=\"wprm-recipe wprm-recipe-template-basic\">\n  <div class=\"wprm-container-float-left\"> \n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-image
