</div>\n  </div> \n  <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Instructions</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-group\">\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions\">\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19654-step-0-0\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Go grab some&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/5568966009/egg-foo-young-ish-spinach-egg-ham-coconut\">Egg Foo Young</a>&nbsp;patties and your jar of&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/quick-pickled-red-onions-paleo-whole30-vegan\">Quick Pickled Red Onions</a>! You can heat the patties in a toaster oven or air fryer at 325°F for 5 minutes or until warmed through. (You can also assemble the sandwiches with cold Egg Foo Young, too!)</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19654-step-0-1\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">In a small bowl, whisk together the mayonnaise and sriracha and slather the sriracha mayonnaise on one side of each piece of bread.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19654-step-0-2\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Pile each sandwich with two paleo&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/5568966009/egg-foo-young-ish-spinach-egg-ham-coconut\">Egg Foo Young patties</a>, two tomato slices, a handful of&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/quick-pickled-red-onions-paleo-whole30-vegan\">Quick Pickled Red Onions</a>, and a lettuce leaf. </span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19654-step-0-3\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Top the remaining pieces of bread on top of the four sandwiches. Slice each St. Paul sandwich in half and enjoy!</span>\n      </div></li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n  </div> \n  <div id=\"wprm-recipe-video-container-19654\" class=\"wprm-recipe-video-container\">\n   <h3 class=\"wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-video-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Video</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-video\"> \n    <div class=\"adthrive-video-player in-post\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"https://schema.org/VideoObject\" data-video-id=\"O9NUFh8d\" data-player-type=\"default\" override-embed=\"default\"> \n     <meta itemprop=\"uploadDate\" content=\"2020-08-11T21:49:18.000Z\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"name\" content=\"St. Paul Sandwich (Paleo, Low Carb, Gluten Free)\" /> \n     <meta itemprop=\"description\" content=\"This St. Paul Sandwich is a paleo, low carb, and gluten-free version of the midwestern Chinese-American classic! Tam","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/St.-Paul-Sandwich-800.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn98@2020_5/2020/08/24/23-01-27-034_88caa2b2af1dadf2.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3439.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn2@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-02-00-294_cf47d96c5209f566.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3373.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn85@2020_5/2020/08/24/23-02-02-802_10a2c7ecdd14db12.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/800eggfooyoungaaaDSC_3228-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn18@2020_5/2020/08/24/23-01-59-248_fa5ace7039c6779c.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3329.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn74@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-01-59-247_da82496773b2db0a.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3411.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn86@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-02-00-364_32b60a82a477ac38.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3421.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn70@2020_1/2020/08/24/23-02-01-711_5a4b7b9ed77e8892.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3504-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn6@2020_3/2020/08/24/23-02-01-889_6f7905d15dc777e7.webp","https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800StPaulSandwichaaDSC_3504-1-150x150.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn14@2020_2/2020/08/24/23-02-02-138_e2b8a2660a90362f.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598310085722},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","title":"Quick Pickled Red Onions (Paleo, Whole30, Vegan)","link":"https://nomnompaleo.com/?p=19596","description":"<p><em>These quick pickled red onions add a tangy crunch to all of your favorite dishes, from burgers to salads! Sweetened only with apple juice, these pickled onions are Whole30-friendly, paleo, and vegan!</em></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19602\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Quick-Pickled-Red-Onions-800.jpg\" alt=\"Someone in a gray apron is using a fork to lift up some quick-pickled red onions from a jar. There is a red banner at the bottom that states that they are paleo, Whole30, gluten-free, and vegan.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Quick-Pickled-Red-Onions-800.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Quick-Pickled-Red-Onions-800-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Quick-Pickled-Red-Onions-800-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Quick-Pickled-Red-Onions-800-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>One of the easiest ways to jazz up a boring dish is to top them with zingy, crunchy pickled onions. It’s my secret weapon for making leftovers taste like bestovers!</p> \n<h2>Cooking Tips For Quick Pickled Onions</h2> \n<h3><strong>Thin rings for the win!&nbsp;</strong></h3> \n<p>Use a mandolin or sharp knife to cut the red onions crosswise into thin rings that are a little less than ¼-inch thick. This way the onion rings will pickle faster, and the thinner slices allow you to control the amount of pickle-y goodness you add to your dishes!</p> \n<h3>Use high quality vinegar and juice!</h3> \n<p>My favorite types of vinegar to use in this recipe are apple cider vinegar and rice wine vinegar. Both are not super sharp and add the right balance of acidity to these pickled onions. In terms of apple juice, my favorite brand is Martinelli’s because it tastes the best in my humble opinion. No apple juice? Grape juice also works!</p> \n<h3>Pickled onions taste best the next day!</h3> \n<p>Although these quick pickled red onions only take a few minutes of hands-on time to throw together and you can eat them as soon as 30 minutes after you dunk them in the brine, I think they taste the best after chilling in the fridge for a few hours. Overnight, the pink onions are pliable and have an acidic bite!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19613\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_4960.jpg\" alt=\"An overhead shot of an open glass jar filled with quick pickled red onions.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_4960.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_4960-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_4960-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>How To Change Them Up!</h2> \n<p>You can pickle other vegetables, like thinly sliced Persian or English cucumbers, slivered carrots, or even thinly sliced daikon! Also, you can add different flavors to the brine like red pepper flakes, crushed garlic cloves, peppercorns, or fresh herbs. Start experimenting with a bunch of different flavor boosters and you’ll end up with a variety of quick pickles!</p> \n<h2>Can You Make Them With a Keto Sweetener?</h2> \n<p>These quick pickled onions are way too tart if you leave out the juice or something sweet to balance out the acidity. Although I don’t use a lot of sugar substitutes, some readers have told me that they have used keto sweeteners like monk fruit, stevia, and erythritol with success. Each sweetener is a different, so add to taste!</p> \n<h2>What Dishes Can You Top With Them?</h2> \n<p>These quick pickled red onions taste great on any savory dish that needs a bracing tangy crunch! I love to throw them on top of <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/nomster-burgers\">burgers</a>, <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/143765161843/pressure-cooker-salsa-chicken-tacos\">tacos</a>, and even salads. Zingy onions are the perfect contrast to heavier meat dishes so they pair perfectly with <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/111934821818/pressure-cooker-kalua-pig\">Instant Pot Kalua Pig</a>, <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/pot-sticker-stir-fry\">Potsticker Stir-Fry (a.k.a. Egg Roll in A Bowl)</a>, and even <a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/7486821187/my-sisters-phenomenal-grilled-green-chicken\">Fiona’s Phenomenal Green Chicken</a>!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19615\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_4989.jpg\" alt=\"A fork pulling out a tangle of quick pickled red onions from a clear glass jar.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_4989.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_4989-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_4989-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>How Long Do They Keep In The Fridge?</h2> \n<p>If you don’t manage to finish these pickles in a couple of days, you can keep them in a sealed container in the fridge for up to a week. These pickles aren’t fermented or pressure canned so mold will grow on them if you keep them longer.</p> \n<h2>Time to Make Quick-Pickled Red Onions!</h2> \n<p><em>Serves 4</em></p> \n<p><strong>Ingredients:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>½ cup apple cider vinegar</li> \n <li>¼ cup apple juice</li> \n <li>½ teaspoon Diamond Crystal kosher salt</li> \n <li>1 medium red onion, thinly sliced</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Equipment:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>All of my recommended kitchen tools are listed <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/shop/nomnompaleo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\"><strong>here</strong></a>.</li> \n <li>The cute Weck jars can be found <strong><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3jJul3P\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">here</a></strong>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Method:</strong></p> \n<p>Combine the apple cider vinegar, juice, and salt in a measuring cup and whisk well.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19603\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4865.jpg\" alt=\"Someone whisking together the vinegar, juice, and salt in a measuring cup to make paleo, Whole30, and vegan quick pickled red onions.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4865.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4865-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4865-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Pack the thin onion slices into a small jar.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19606\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4883.jpg\" alt=\"Someone adding thin red onion slices in an open Weck jar.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4883.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4883-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4883-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Pour the brine over the onions and use a fork to submerge the onions completely.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19607\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4931.jpg\" alt=\"A fork pressing red onion slices in the brine to make Whole30 quick pickled red onions.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4931.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4931-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4931-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /><br /> Cover and set aside in the refrigerator for at least 30 minutes before diving in!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19610\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4940.jpg\" alt=\"Two hands holding a clear glass jar filled with quick pickled red onions.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4940.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4940-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800PickledOnionsaaDSC_4940-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>These quick pickled red onions should keep for about a week in the fridge in an airtight container. Put them on all the things!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-19611\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_5025.jpg\" alt=\"A fork removing quick pickled red onions from an open clear glass jar.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_5025.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_5025-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_5025-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/800QuickPickledOnionsaaDSC_5025-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<hr /> \n<p><em>Looking for more recipe ideas? href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/foodforhumanscookbook\">Nom Nom Paleo: Food for Humans</a>&nbsp;(Andrews McMeel Publishing 2013) and&nbsp;<a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/readyornotcookbook\">Ready or 07:01:25","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 07:01:25","title":"Berry Snack Cake (Paleo, Gluten Free)","link":"https://nomnompaleo.com/?p=19773","description":"<p><em>This simple and delicious Berry Snack Cake is the perfect back-to-school paleo and gluten-free treat! Both kids and adults love this snack cake because you can eat it without utensils and no one will suspect that it’s free of grains and refined sugar!</em></p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20232\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Berry-Snack-Cake-800.jpg\" alt=\"A closeup shot of a slice of berry snack cake topped with keto confectioners sugar on a white plate. The red banner on the bottom says paleo, gluten-free, and grain-free.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Berry-Snack-Cake-800.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Berry-Snack-Cake-800-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Berry-Snack-Cake-800-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Berry-Snack-Cake-800-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>This berry snack cake has a tender crumb dotted with tangy berries and just the right amount of sweetness from maple or coconut sugar! Also, it passed the test with my picky gluten-eating in-laws, so you know this snacking cake is a winner!</p> \n<h2>It’s Paleo, Gluten-Free, and Grain-Free!</h2> \n<p>I don’t make paleo desserts often, but when I do, I make sure they are worth all of the testing. This berry snack cake tastes amazing and the only flours used are almond flour and cassava flour. As I’ve told you in the past, I’m not a paleo baking expert, so I’m not sure if you can use an egg substitute or use another flour in place of the two used in this recipe. Please let me know in the comments section below if you have success with any ingredient substitutions!</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20265\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7827.jpg\" alt=\"An overhead shot of paleo and gluten free berry snack cake right out of the oven.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7827.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7827-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7827-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7827-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<h2>Can you Make This Keto?</h2> \n<p>Maybe? I suspect you can use a keto granulated sugar (like <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3atHWs1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Swerve</a>) &nbsp;in place of the maple or coconut sugar, but I haven’t tried it myself. Also, you can probably use mostly almond flour to decrease the carbs as well. However, I’m not sure of the exact proportions so if you do try it, please let folks know in the comments below how it turns out!</p> \n<h2>Can You Use Other Fruit?</h2> \n<p>Definitely! You can substitute the berries with almost any other sliced up fruit. Peaches, nectarines, plums, mango, or canned pineapple work great! If you’re using a hard fruit, like an apple, slice it thin so it can cook in the time the batter sets up. Frozen fruit will also work but it will take longer to bake and the finished cake will be wetter.</p> \n<h2>More Grab-and-Go Paleo Dessert Ideas!</h2> \n<p>If you’re looking for more portable paleo dessert recipes, here are some of my favorites:</p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/chocolate-cherry-paleo-granola\">Cherry Chocolate Granola</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/easy-cinnamon-rolls-in-a-muffin-pan-paleo-gluten-free\">Easy Cinnamon Rolls in A Muffin Pan</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/146982443503/liar-balls\">Liar Balls</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/pbj-energy-balls\">PB&amp;J Energy Balls</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/paleo-pumpkin-muffins\">Pumpkin Muffins</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/post/140290900313/the-worlds-easiest-cookies\">The World’s Easiest Cookies</a></li> \n</ul> \n<h2>Let’s Make a Paleo and Gluten Free Berry Snack Cake!</h2> \n<p><em>Serves 9</em></p> \n<p><strong>Ingredients:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>Avocado oil spray or ghee</li> \n <li>1 cup (112 grams) finely ground almond flour</li> \n <li>¾ cup (96 grams) cassava flour (I use <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2Y7LFXo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Otto’s cassava flour</a>)</li> \n <li>1 teaspoon ground cinnamon</li> \n <li>½ teaspoon baking soda</li> \n <li>½ teaspoon Diamond Crystal kosher salt</li> \n <li>½ teaspoon ground cardamom</li> \n <li>½ cup (112 grams) ghee or coconut oil, softened</li> \n <li>⅔ cup (96 grams) maple sugar or coconut sugar</li> \n <li>2 large eggs</li> \n <li>⅓ cup full-fat coconut milk</li> \n <li>2 teaspoons grated lime zest</li> \n <li>1 teaspoon lime juice</li> \n <li>1 teaspoon vanilla extract</li> \n <li>1½ cups (213 grams) blackberries, blueberries, strawberries, and/or raspberries</li> \n <li>1 tablespoon <a href=\"https://amzn.to/320SMBJ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">keto confectioners sugar</a> (optional)</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Equipment:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>All of my recommended kitchen tools are listed <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/shop/nomnompaleo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\"><strong>here</strong></a>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p><strong>Method:</strong></p> \n<p>Heat oven to 350°F with the rack in the middle. Lightly grease the sides and bottom of an 8-­inch square metal baking pan with avocado oil or ghee. Make a sling out of parchment paper to line the bottom and hang over the sides.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20234\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6610.jpg\" alt=\"Someone placing a parchment paper sling in a greased 8 by 8 inch square metal baking cake pan.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6610.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6610-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6610-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>In medium bowl, whisk together flours, cinnamon, baking soda, salt, and cardamom. Set aside.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20235\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6574.jpg\" alt=\"Whisking the dry ingredients for a paleo and gluten free berry snack cake.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6574.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6574-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6574-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Plop the softened ghee and maple sugar in the bowl of a stand mixer (or in a large bowl if you are using a hand mixer).</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20237\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6643.jpg\" alt=\"A stand mixer bowl has ghee and maple sugar in it, along with the paddle attachment.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6643.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6643-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6643-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Use the paddle attachment to blend the mixture on medium-high speed for 3 to 5 minutes or until lighter in color and fluffy.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20238\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6704.jpg\" alt=\"The creamed ghee and maple sugar is now a pale yellow color in the inside of a bowl of a stand mixer.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6704.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6704-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6704-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Scrape down the sides of the bowl and add the eggs, coconut milk, lime zest and juice, and vanilla.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20239\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6768a.jpg\" alt=\"Adding lime juice and vanilla to the wet ingredients in the stand mixer.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6768a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6768a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6768a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Beat the mixture on medium speed for 30 seconds or until combined. Next, add half the flour mixture and beat on low speed until combined.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20240\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6828a.jpg\" alt=\"On the left is the wet ingredients in the stand mixer. On the right, someone is adding half the dry ingredients to the wet ingredients in the mixer.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6828a.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6828a-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6828a-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Slowly add the rest of the flour and mix until incorporated.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20242\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6909.jpg\" alt=\"The berry snack cake batter is ready to mix in the berries.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6909.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6909-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6909-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Scrape down the sides of the bowl and mix in any dry flour with a spatula. Pour in the berries…</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20243\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6954.jpg\" alt=\"Adding blueberries and raspberries to a mixing bowl to make paleo berry snack cake.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6954.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6954-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6954-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>…and carefully fold them in the thick batter.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20244\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6989.jpg\" alt=\"A red silicone spatula is folding in the berries in the berry snack cake batter.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6989.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6989-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_6989-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Transfer the batter to the parchment-lined baking pan and smooth the top.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20245\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7039.jpg\" alt=\"A red silicone spatula is smoothing the top of berry snack cake batter in a parchment lined square metal pan.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7039.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7039-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7039-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Pop the pan in the oven and bake until the cake is golden brown and a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean, about 30-35 minutes.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20246\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7541.jpg\" alt=\"A golden brown berry snack cake is being removed out of the oven.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7541.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7541-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7541-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Cool the cake in the pan on a cooling rack.&nbsp;Cut the cake into nine squares…</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20247\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7914.jpg\" alt=\"Someone cutting a paleo and gluten-free berry snack cake into nine evenly sized pieces.\" width=\"800\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7914.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7914-300x200.jpg 300w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_7914-768x512.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>…and top with keto confectioner’s sugar if desired.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20248\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8127.jpg\" alt=\"Someone adding sifted keto confectioners sugar onto the paleo berry snack cakes\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8127.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8127-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8127-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8127-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>Store leftover cake in a sealed container or wrapped in plastic wrap in the fridge for up to 4 days or in the freezer for up to 4 months.</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-20249\" src=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8037.jpg\" alt=\"Someone holding a square slice of paleo and gluten-free berry snack cake.\" width=\"800\" height=\"1200\" srcset=\"https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8037.jpg 800w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8037-200x300.jpg 200w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8037-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://nomnompaleo.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/800SnackCakeaaDSC_8037-750x1125.jpg 750w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p> \n<p>But something tells me you won’t have very many leftovers!</p> \n<hr /> \n<p><em>Looking for more recipe ideas? wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none\" style=\"\">Instructions</h3>\n   <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-group\">\n    <ul class=\"wprm-recipe-instructions\">\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19774-step-0-0\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Heat oven to 350°F with the rack in the middle. Lightly grease the sides and bottom of an 8-­inch square metal baking pan with avocado oil or ghee. Make a sling out of parchment paper to line the bottom and hang over the sides.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19774-step-0-1\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">In medium bowl, whisk together flours, cinnamon, baking soda, salt, and cardamom. Set aside.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19774-step-0-2\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Plop the softened ghee and maple sugar in the bowl of a stand mixer (or in a large bowl if you are using a hand mixer). Use the paddle attachment to blend the mixture on medium-high speed for 3 to 5 minutes or until lighter in color and fluffy.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19774-step-0-3\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Scrape down the sides of the bowl and add the eggs, coconut milk, lime zest and juice, and vanilla. Beat the mixture on medium speed for 30 seconds or until combined.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19774-step-0-4\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Next, add half the flour mixture and beat on low speed until combined. Slowly add the rest of the flour and mix until incorporated. Scrape down the sides of the bowl and mix in any dry flour with a spatula. </span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19774-step-0-5\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Carefully fold the berries into the batter.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19774-step-0-6\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Transfer the batter to the parchment-lined baking pan and smooth the top.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19774-step-0-7\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Pop the pan in the oven and bake until the cake is golden brown and a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean, about 30-35 minutes.</span>\n      </div></li>\n     <li id=\"wprm-recipe-19774-step-0-8\" class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction\" style=\"list-style-type: decimal;\">\n      <div class=\"wprm-recipe-instruction-text\" style=\"margin-bottom: 5px\">\n       <span style=\"display: block;\">Cool the cake in the pan on a cooling rack.&nbsp;Cut the cake into nine squares and serve as is or top with keto confectioners sugar.</span>\n      </div></li>\n
